  - split: 8
    text: "千百年前玄门仙师白闻清广纳徒生，传授学说，其弟子中不乏才情绝艳之人，受此影响，玄门思想进一步扩大。纵历经风波战乱，玄门依旧是如今的三大教派之一。玄门门派太初剑宗、清玉门、御虚门等皆有自己的门生弟子所有玄门弟子，皆称为羽士。\\n若想成为羽士，需寻得羽士教导才行。羽士数量众多，各个城镇与玄门门派中皆有他们行动的踪迹，甚至有身份更高的隐士、闲云等，也可向他们求教。各大门派和江湖中也有羽士。(893,1392)处便有羽士。"
    translated: "Thousands of years ago, the Xuanmen Taoist practitioner Bai Wenqing broadened his discipleship and imparted his teachings. Among his students were individuals with extraordinary talent and beauty. Influenced by him, Xuanmen philosophy further expanded. Despite enduring storms and upheavals, Xuanmen remains one of today's three major sects. The Xuanmen sect includes the Primordial Sword Sect, Pure Jade Gate, Imperial Void Gate, among others, each with their own disciples. All disciples of Xuanmen are referred to as Taoist practitioners.\\nIf one wishes to become a Taoist practitioner, they must seek guidance from a Taoist practitioner. There are many Taoist practitioners, and their presence can be found in various towns, among the xuanmen sects, as well as among recluses and idle immortals who have higher status; teachings can also be sought from them. There are Taoist practitioners within major sects and across the Jianghu as well. (893,1392) is a place where you will find Taoist practitioners."

    translated: "When the Secret Art reaches a plateau, mastering the special skill White Deer and Green Cliff allows one to advance to the level of hermit."
